This document is long, difficult to read and only gives small partial examples. This app creates complete Pdf sample files and allows you concentrating on specific aspects a Pdf text. It offers five classes of samples:\r\n\r\n1. Simple text. The smallest Pdf file consists of a single line. This class offers Pdf samples containing a single short line, a single long line (requiring wrapping it) and combinations of short and long lines.\r\n\r\n2. Markup text. The table samples show a table with or without border lines, with or without background colors and with or without merged cells. This is text in a different language and represented by an alphabet, different from the Latin alphabet. Examples are Greek and Japanese.
